	OutputLine(NULL, "　…あぁ、親の存在が邪魔臭い…。",
		   NULL, "...Ah, my parents being here is such a bother...", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　昭和５６年を、この世界では運良く潜り抜けられたと思ったら、私が元の世界へ帰るのを邪魔までするなんて…！",
		   NULL, "Just when I thought I'd been lucky that they made it through the year 1981, they're getting in the way of me returning to the final world...!", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode) == 0) { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　祭具殿の中で、羽入の名をあれだけ大声で呼んでいたから、気配を悟られてしまったのだろう。",
		   NULL, "In the storehouse, I'd been shouting Hanyuu's name pretty loudly, so he'd probably noticed.", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　…明日から本格的に祭具殿の中を調べるが、二度と父に見つからないよう、細心の注意を払う必要があるだろう。",
		   NULL, "...I would investigate the storehouse for real tomorrow, but I'd have to take extreme caution so that my father didn't find me.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	FadeOutBGM( 0, 1000, FALSE );
	DrawScene( "bg/moon", 1000 );
	PlayBGM( 0, "t2", 120, 0 );

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　…深夜、さんざん叩かれてお尻が腫れ上がり、仰向けに眠れない布団の上で、……私は枕を噛みながら、もう一度だけ泣き、",
		   NULL, "...In the middle of the night, unable to sleep face-up on my futon because of my rear end swelled up from all the spanking... I bit my pillow and cried again......", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLine(NULL, "………自分の成すべき事にもう一度思いを馳せるのだった……。",
		   NULL, " then thought back over what I had to do...", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　自分の部屋なのに。",
		   NULL, "This was my room.", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　自分の布団なのに。",
		   NULL, "This was my futon.", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　…ここは私が寝るべきところじゃない。",
		   NULL, "...But this wasn't where I was supposed to sleep.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　私が本当に帰るべき布団は、…倉庫小屋の２階を改造した狭い家で、……沙都子と私の布団が並んでいるところ。",
		   NULL, "The futon I was supposed to go home to... was in the small house on the second floor of the renovated warehouse... the one next to Satoko's.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　でもこの世界ではきっと、あそこは未だに青年団の会議所のままなのだ。",
		   NULL, "But in this world, the youth group was probably still using it as a meeting place.", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　…だから、そこに私の布団があったりはしない。",

	ClearMessage();

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　なら、……私はこの世界の、どこの布団で眠ればいいの………。",

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　せっかく勝ち取った未来を、下らない不注意で台無しにしたことへの、…報い。",
		   NULL, "Punishment... for doing something stupid and careless, bringing the future we all won to nothing.", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode) == 0) { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

	OutputLine(NULL, "　羽入を呼び寄せるために、それを邪魔している何かを見つけなければならない。",
		   NULL, "I needed to find what was keeping Hanyuu away so I could call her here.", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode) == 0) { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　それには相当の労力を要するだろう。",
		   NULL, "It would take a lot of effort.", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));

	OutputLine(NULL, "　そのためにも、今は鋭気を養って休息を取るべきで、涙を流すなど時間と体力の無駄でしかないはず。",

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　……わかっていても、……私は寝付くまで、枕を涙で濡らし続けるのだった………。",

	ClearMessage();
